INSERT INTO CHROMOSOME_SIZE SELECT REF_GEN as GEN, REF_CHR as CHR, max(END_BP) as SIZE from CONSENSUS where REF_GEN = 'RACA:APCF:300K' group by REF_GEN, REF_CHR;
